# Runs.txt

This file lists every local run from `outputs/run_registry/local_outputs_inventory.csv` with only known values shown.

Inventory rows: 417
Generated from uploaded run registry + local inventory metadata.

Legend:
- exact = manifest or exact launcher is available.
- reconstructed = best-effort from known local metadata; not guaranteed exact.
- not reproducible = insufficient metadata to reconstruct a command.
- UNKNOWN values are intentionally omitted from each run block instead of printing long lists of UNKNOWN fields.

IMPORTANT: Commands are for documentation/copy-paste only. Do not use contaminated/debug runs as final thesis evidence.
